                       Our private bedroom is bright, spacious and quiet. Located on the 2nd floor of our Townhouse in safe and residential Burbank, it receives light throughout the day. There is also a bedside table and reading light, floor-to-ceiling mirrors, a large closet for your clothes and belongings, a lock on the door and complete shut out blinds. There is also storage space for your bags. Our townhouse is a true oasis of calm, and well connected to Los Angeles and the San Fernando Valley. We're housed in a block of Townhouses, and being at the very front facing the street we have some lovely views of the mountains and the valley, as well as receiving light in all areas of the house. The Townhouse is modern and comfortable, with wooden floors on the first floor and carpet on the second floor. When you're staying here it's hard to believe you are just a few miles away from all the major studios and shopping and entertainment options available.

                      <div data-reactid="2087">
                       My property in L.A./ lower Glendale consists of many adorable cottages with a central courtyard. All the same size/amenities. It has become a boutique extended stay of sorts. Most of my guests are here for at least a month and some over a year... I weave shorter stays in and out of the longer ones. For that reason I operate a master calendar. If you are flexible as to which cottage, quiet, communicative and a non-smoker...That's GREAT! Please let me know you are flexible as to which cottage with your first communication so I will know if I can accept your reservation. QUEEN BED. NO SMOKING or Animals ALLOWED. Adorable! Stylish, renovated, one bedroom Cottage Style Suite located in the Southern part of Glendale, right next to Atwater Village, minutes away from downtown LA, Silverlake, Los Feliz, and Hollywood. Also minutes from Burbank, the Valley and Eaglerock. In a word it is extremely "central". On a tree lined residential street, the courtyard itself is loaded with sun and has lovely large palm trees. This cottage is "house like" with both a front and back door. Though there are some common walls, there is no one above or below. It has hardwood floors throughout and is 1920's renovated with Design in mind. Great for singles, couples, business professionals, students, and tourists. All furniture and home items are solely for the use of our guests. Laundry on premises. The Kitchen is fully stocked with microwave, stove, toaster, utensils, dishes, pots and pans. Each suite comes with it's own full size ironing board, iron and hair dryer. Included is a large, flat screen TV which is equipped with a streaming media device and an HDTV antenna allowing you to access quite a many local channels. GREAT Wi-Fi! It even works in the courtyard. Guests will enjoy a Spanish style courtyard, with adirondack chairs, chaise lounges, tables and chairs. Silverlake and Los Feliz are 4 miles away, Hollywood is 6 miles away and 8 miles to downtown Los Angeles. Studio close, both for Burbank and Hollywood. The city of Glendale boasts a VERY low crime rate, even though it is minutes from Los Angeles. Also close to Silverlake, Burbank and Atwater. You can walk to the all new Americana, which has lots of restaurants, bars, name brand stores, including Katsuya Bar and The Cheese Cake Factory. Ralph's and Trader Joe's are 1 mile away as well as Griffith Park, the home of The Griffith Park Observatory. Within thirty minutes of the mountains, beaches, and so much more. Close to the 5 and 134 freeways, as well as public transportation. We can't wait to meet you! ~There is a 12% tax in the city of Glendale for short term rentals. Any stay under one month will be assessed this tax. Payment is made directly to host and must be completed on or before entry. Nightly fee is assessed for additional guests beyond 2. Extra person would be sleeping on the sofa and the sofa does not pull out into a bed. No Pets and NO Smoking allowed. The finalization of reservations is contingent upon returning rental agreement and copy of ID within 24 hours of receipt. Guests will receive this agreement by email after booking.
